title: "Mini HoTT library in Agda"
date: "2018-07-05"
categories: type-theory
toc: true
agda: true
---

This is my attempt to collect in just one-file, a basic overview of HoTT in Agda.
This source code was type-checked by Agda 2.5.4.

{: .references }

  - https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/
  - https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT (`--without-K`):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="439" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="443" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="451" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="463" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="468" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="473" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="480" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="495" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="501" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="503" href="Agda.Primitive.html#408" class="Postulate">Level</a> <a id="509" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="511" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a><a id="515" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="517" href="Agda.Primitive.html#611" class="Primitive">lzero</a><a id="522" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="524" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">_⊔_</a> <a id="528" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="531" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#531" class="Function">_</a> <a id="533" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="535" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="539" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Universes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword `Set`. It uses `Type` instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="812" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="819" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#819" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="829" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="838" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="904" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="970" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>

Types
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

### Unit

The unit type is defined as record so that we also get the η-rule definitionally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1873" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
<a id="1931" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
<a id="1947" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="⊤"></a><a id="1954" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1954" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1956" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1958" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1109" class="Function">Type₀</a> <a id="1964" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="1972" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="⊤.★"></a><a id="1984" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1984" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="unit"></a><a id="1987" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1987" class="Function">unit</a> <a id="1992" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1994" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1984" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="1997" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="2001" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> UNIT <a id="2014" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1954" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="2016" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

### Σ-types

Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be
constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum
of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in
full generality, at each universe.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2359" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2366" class="Number">60</a> <a id="2369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2458" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>

### Π-types
Shorter notation for Π-types.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Π"></a><a id="2631" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2631" class="Function">Π</a> <a id="2633" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2635" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2637" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2638" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2638" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2641" href="{% endraw %}{% link * Booleans can be defined by using a coproduct.

### Natural numbers

Natural numbers are the initial algebra for a constant and a
successor function. The BUILTIN declaration allows us to use
natural numbers in arabic notation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3472" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ"></a><a id="3477" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3477" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3479" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3481" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1109" class="Function">Type₀</a> <a id="3487" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ.zero"></a><a id="3495" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="3500" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3502" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3477" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="ℕ.succ"></a><a id="3506" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3506" class="InductiveConstructor">succ</a> <a id="3511" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3513" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3477" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3515" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3517" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3477" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="Nat"></a><a id="3520" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3520" class="Function">Nat</a> <a id="3524" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3526" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3477" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

### Common functions

#### Identity function
The identity function with implicit type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="id"></a><a id="3668" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3668" class="Function">id</a> <a id="3671" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3673" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3675" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3676" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3676" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3677" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3679" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3680" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3680" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3682" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3684" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3689" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3676" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3690" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3692" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3694" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3680" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3696" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3698" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3680" class="Bound">A</a>

The identity function on a type `A` is `idf A`.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="idf"></a><a id="3782" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3782" class="Function">idf</a> <a id="3786" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3788" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3790" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3791" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3791" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="3793" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3796" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3796" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3798" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3800" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3805" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3791" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="3807" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3809" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3811" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3812" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3796" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3814" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3816" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3796" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3817" class="Symbol">)</a>

#### Composition

A more sophisticated composition function that can handle dependent functions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4133" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="4140" class="Number">80</a> <a id="4143" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4147" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a>
<a id="_∘_"></a><a id="4147" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4147" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a> <a id="4151" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4153" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="4155" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4156" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4156" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="4159" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a> <a id="4162" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4162" class="Bound">ℓₖ</a><a id="4164" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="4170" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4171" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4171" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4173" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4175" href="{% ### Homogeneous Equality

The Identity type is defined as an inductive type. Its induction principle
is the J-eliminator.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5154" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="5160" class="Number">30</a> <a id="5163" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5173" class="Datatype Operator">_==_</a>

  <a id="5786" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5787" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5787" class="Bound">a&#39;</a> <a id="5790" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5792" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5710" class="Bound">A</a><a id="5793" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5796" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5796" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="5798" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5800" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5787" class="Bound">a&#39;</a> <a id="5803" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5173" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="5806" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5724" class="Bound">a</a><a id="5807" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5809" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5811" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5732" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="5813" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5787" class="Bound">a&#39;</a> <a id="5816" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5796" class="Bound">p</a>

### PathOver

Let be `A : Type`, `a₁, a₂ : A`, `C : A → Type`, `c₁ : C a₁` and `c₂ : C a₂`.
Using the same notation from {% cite hottbook %}, one of the definitions for the
Pathover type is as the shorthand for the path between the transport along a
path `α : a₁ = a₂` of the point `c₁ : C a₁` and the point `c₂` in the fiber `C
a₂`. That is, a pathover is a term that inhabit the type `transport C α c₁ = c₂`
also denoted by `PathOver C α c₁ c₂`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6665" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="PathOver"></a><a id="6670" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6670" class="Datatype">PathOver</a> <a id="6679" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6680" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6680" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="6683" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6683" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6685" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6687" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6688" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6688" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6690" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6692" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6696" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6680" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="6698" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6700" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6701" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6701" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="6703" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6705" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6688" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6707" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6709" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6714" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6683" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6716" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6718" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6719" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6719" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="6722" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6724" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6688" class="Bound">A</a><a id="6725" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6727" class="Symbol">:</a>
      <a id="6735" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6736" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6736" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="6739" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6741" ## Equational Reasoning

Equational reasoning is a way to write readable chains of equalities.
The idea is that you can write the following:

{% raw %}
```agda
  t : a == e
  t = a =⟨ p ⟩
      b =⟨ q ⟩
      c =⟨ r ⟩
      d =⟨ s ⟩
      e ∎
```
{% endraw %}

where `p` is a path from `a` to `b`, `q` is a path from `b` to `c`, and so on.
You often have to apply some equality in some context, for instance `p` could be
`ap ctx thm` where `thm` is the interesting theorem used to prove that `a` is
equal to `b`, and `ctx` is the context. [More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L270).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7563" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="7570" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7570" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7590" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7591" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7591" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7593" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7595" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7596" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7596" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7598" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7600" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7605" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7591" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7607" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7609" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7618" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="7625" class="Number">2</a> <a id="7627" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7636" class="Function Operator">_==⟨⟩_</a>

<a id="7926" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="7931" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7570" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7951" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

### Equality

Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this
is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this
is the symmetric property of equality.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="inv"></a><a id="8237" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8237" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8241" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8243" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8245" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8245" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8246" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8248" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8249" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8249" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8251" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8253" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8258" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8245" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8259" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8262" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8263" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8263" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8265" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8265" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8267" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8269" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8249" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8270" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8272" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8274" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8263" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8276" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5173" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8279" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8265" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8281" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8283" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8265" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5173" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8288" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8263" class="Bound">a</a>

<a id="_⁻¹"></a><a id="8305" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8305" class="Function Operator">_⁻¹</a> <a id="8309" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8311" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8237" class="Function">inv</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions
preserve equalities.

#### Associativity of composition

Properties of function composition.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="8636" class="Comment">-- Left associativity</a>
<a id="∘-lassoc"></a><a id="8658" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8658" class="Function">∘-lassoc</a>
  <a id="8669" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8671" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="8673" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8674" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8674" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8675" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8677" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8678" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8678" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8680" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8680" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8682" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8682" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="8684" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8684" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="8686" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8688" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8693" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8674" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8694" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="8698" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8700" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8701" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8701" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="8703" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8705" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8682" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="8707" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8709" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8684" class="Bound">D</a><a id="8710" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8712" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8714" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8715" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8715" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="8717" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8719" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8680" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8721" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8723" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8682" class="Bound">C</a><a id="8724" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8726" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8728" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8729" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8729" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8731" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8733" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8678" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8735" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8737" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8680" class="Bound">B</a><a id="8738" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Properties on the groupoid

Some properties on the groupoid structure of equalities

<a id="10098" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="10103" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9121" class="Module">·-Properties</a> <a id="10116" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

    <a id="15119" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15121" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15122" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15122" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15124" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15126" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15127" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15127" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="15129" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15131" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15073" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15132" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15134" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15088" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15138" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15127" class="Bound">a</a><a id="15139" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15141" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15143" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15144" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15144" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="15146" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15148" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15106" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="15150" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5173" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="15153" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15108" class="Bound">b</a><a id="15154" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15360" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="15367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15367" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="15376" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15377" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15377" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="15380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15380" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15382" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15384" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15385" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15385" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15387" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15389" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15394" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15377" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="15396" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15398" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15399" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15401" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15403" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15385" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15405" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15407" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15412" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15380" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15414" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15416" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="15424" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="15502" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="15542" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15542" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15551" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15553" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15554" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15554" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15556" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15556" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15560" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15562" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15562" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15564" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15566" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15385" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15567" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15569" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15571" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15399" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15573" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15562" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15574" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15577" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15579" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15584" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15585" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15377" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="15588" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15590" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15380" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15592" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15596" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15542" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15605" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15605" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15607" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15607" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15609" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15611" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15612" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15612" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15616" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15385" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15617" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15619" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15621" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15605" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15623" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15612" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15625" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5173" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="15628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15607" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15630" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15612" class="Bound">x</a>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

<a id="16989" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="16994" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#16769" class="Module">Naturality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Fibers

Contractible types with a center of contraction.

  <a id="18327" class="Comment">-- Each point is on the fiber of its image</a>

  <a id="18422" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18372" class="Function">fib-image</a> <a id="18432" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18433" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18433" class="Bound">f</a><a id="18434" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18436" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18437" class="Bound">a</a><a id="18438" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18440" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18442" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18437" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="18444" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2458" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18446" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5308" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="18451" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18433" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18454" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18437" class="Bound">a</a><a id="18455" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Contractible types

## Equivalence

  <a id="18916" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DefinitionOfEquivalence"></a><a id="18923" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18923" class="Module">DefinitionOfEquivalence</a> <a id="18947" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18948" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18948" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18951" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18951" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18953" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18955" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18956" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18956" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18958" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18960" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18965" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18948" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="18967" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18969" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18970" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18970" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18972" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18974" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18979" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18951" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18981" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18983" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="18993" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="19061" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="19126" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>

    <a id="19189" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19143" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="19200" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19200" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19202" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19204" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19205" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19205" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="19207" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19209" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18970" class="Bound">B</a><a id="19210" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19212" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18735" class="Function">isContr</a> <a id="19222" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19223" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18099" class="Function">fib</a> <a id="19227" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19200" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19205" class="Bound">b</a><a id="19230" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="20571" class="Comment">-- Application of an homotopy</a>

  <a id="20675" class="Comment">-- The axiom of function extensionality postulates that the</a>
  <a id="20737" class="Comment">-- application of homotopies is an equivalence.</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22850" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="22857" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22857" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="22874" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22875" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22875" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="22878" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22878" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22880" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22882" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22883" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22883" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22885" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22887" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22892" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22875" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="22894" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22896" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22897" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22897" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="22899" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22901" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22906" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22878" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22908" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22910" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22919" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>

## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23997" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="24004" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24004" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="24022" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24023" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24023" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24024" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24026" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24035" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="24106" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="24144" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24144" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="24150" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24152" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24153" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24153" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24155" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24157" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24162" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24023" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24163" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24165" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24167" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24172" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24023" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="24176" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24144" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="24182" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24182" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24184" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24186" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24187" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24187" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24189" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24189" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="24191" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24193" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24182" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24194" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24196" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24198" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24199" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24187" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24201" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5173" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24204" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24189" class="Bound">b</a><a id="24205" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24207" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2983" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="24209" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1705" class="Function">¬</a> <a id="24211" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24212" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24187" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5173" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24217" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24189" class="Bound">b</a><a id="24218" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24223" class="Comment">-- The product of types with decidable equality is a type with</a>
  <a id="24288" class="Comment">-- decidable equality.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEqProd"></a><a id="24313" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24313" class="Function">decEqProd</a> <a id="24323" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24325" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24326" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24326" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24328" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24328" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24330" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24332" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24337" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24023" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24338" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24340" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24342" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24144" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="24348" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24326" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24350" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24352" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24144" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="24358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24328" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24360" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24362" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24144" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="24368" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24326" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24371" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2807" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24328" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24374" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="24707" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24712" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24004" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24942" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="24949" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24949" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="24962" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24971" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="25040" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>

  <a id="25488" class="Comment">-- The product of propositions is itself a proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="25546" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25546" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="25558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25560" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="25562" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25563" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25563" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="25566" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25566" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="25568" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25570" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25572" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25573" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25573" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25577" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="25582" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25563" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="25584" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25586" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25588" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25589" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25589" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25591" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25593" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="25598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25566" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="25600" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="25616" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25618" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25055" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="25625" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25573" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25055" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="25636" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25589" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25638" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25640" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25055" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="25647" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25648" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25573" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25650" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2807" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="25652" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25589" class="Bound">B</a><a id="25653" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="25717" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25722" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24949" class="Module">Propositions</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25929" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="25936" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25936" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="25941" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25950" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="26021" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="26897" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="HLevels"></a><a id="26904" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#26904" class="Module">HLevels</a> <a id="26912" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="26921" class="Comment">-- Propositions are Sets.</a>

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

  <a id="28679" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28636" class="Function">isProp-≃</a> <a id="28688" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28688" class="Bound">eq</a> <a id="28691" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28691" class="Bound">prop</a> <a id="28696" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28696" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28698" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28698" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="28700" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="28706" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7873" class="Function Operator">begin</a>

<a id="28908" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28913" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28128" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="29157" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="29164" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29164" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="29177" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29178" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29178" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="29181" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29181" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="29183" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="29185" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29186" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29186" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="29188" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29190" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="29195" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29178" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="29197" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="29199" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29200" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29200" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="29202" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29204" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="29209" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29181" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="29211" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="29213" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="29222" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>

  <a id="31691" class="Comment">-- Half-adjointness implies equivalence.</a>
  <a id="Halfadjoints.ishae-≃"></a><a id="31734" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31734" class="Function">ishae-≃</a> <a id="31742" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31744" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31745" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31745" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="31747" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31749" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29186" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31751" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31753" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29200" class="Bound">B</a><a id="31754" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31756" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31758" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29260" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="31764" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31745" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="31766" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31768" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29186" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31770" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19483" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="31772" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29200" class="Bound">B</a>
  <a id="31776" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31734" class="Function">ishae-≃</a> <a id="31784" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31784" class="Bound">ishaef</a> <a id="31791" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31793" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="31795" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2458" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31797" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31798" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29495" class="Function">ishae-contr</a> <a id="31810" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="31812" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31784" class="Bound">ishaef</a><a id="31818" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="31821" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="31826" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#29164" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="31839" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="32006" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="32013" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#32013" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="32027" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32028" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#32028" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="32031" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#32031" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="32033" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32035" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32036" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#32036" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32038" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32040" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="32045" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#32028" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="32047" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32049" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32050" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#32050" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="32052" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32054" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="32059" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#32031" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="32061" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32063" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="37914" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="37919" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#36456" class="Module">SigmaEquivalence</a> <a id="37936" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="38118" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Univalence"></a><a id="38125" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38125" class="Module">Univalence</a> <a id="38136" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="38145" class="Comment">-- Voevodsky&#39;s Univalence Axiom.</a>
  <a id="38180" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="UnivalenceAxiom"></a><a id="38187" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38187" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="38203" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38204" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38204" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="38205" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38207" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="38210" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38210" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="38212" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1012" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="38219" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38204" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="38220" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38222" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="Univalence.UnivalenceAxiom.idtoeqv"></a><a id="38232" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38232" class="Function">idtoeqv</a> <a id="38240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38242" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="38244" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5173" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="38247" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38210" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="38249" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="38251" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="38253" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19483" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="38255" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38210" class="Bound">B</a>

      <a id="38286" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10256" class="Function">transport</a> <a id="38297" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="38300" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38300" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="38302" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="38304" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38300" class="Bound">x</a><a id="38305" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38307" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38269" class="Bound">p</a><a id="38308" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="38316" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38317" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10256" class="Function">transport</a> <a id="38327" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="38330" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38330" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="38332" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="38334" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38330" class="Bound">x</a><a id="38335" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38337" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38338" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8237" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="38342" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38269" class="Bound">p</a><a id="38343" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38345" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2458" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="38347" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38348" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14044" class="Function">transport-inv-l</a> <a id="38364" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38269" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="38366" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2458" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="38368" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14211" class="Function">transport-inv-r</a> <a id="38384" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38269" class="Bound">p</a><a id="38385" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="38922" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="38927" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#38187" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="38943" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Somme lemmas about Univelance


{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="39022" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="39025" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="39064" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="39125" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="39174" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="39193" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="39208" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="39273" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="39326" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="39344" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="39355" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="39358" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="39430" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="39455" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="39551" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="39572" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="39587" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="39694" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="39799" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="39878" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="39954" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="40037" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="40060" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="40071" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="40086" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="40172" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="40201" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="40220" class="Comment">--             π₁ (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ π₁ (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="40306" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="40416" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="40504" class="Comment">--             π₁ (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="40546" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="40562" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="40565" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="40599" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="40679" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="40699" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="40714" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="40784" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="40849" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="40898" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="40916" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="40927" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="40930" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
<a id="41005" class="Comment">--     ua-inv α =</a>
<a id="41023" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="41038" class="Comment">--         ua (invEqv α)                       ==⟨ ap (_· ua (invEqv α)) (inv (·-linv (ua α))) ⟩</a>
<a id="41135" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · ua α · ua (invEqv α)   ==⟨ ·-assoc (inv (ua α)) _ _ ⟩</a>
<a id="41213" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · (ua α · ua (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap (inv (ua α) ·_) (ua-inv-r α) ⟩</a>
<a id="41298" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · refl _                 ==⟨ inv (·-runit (inv ((ua α)))) ⟩</a>
<a id="41380" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α)</a>
<a id="41402" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="41413" class="Comment">--   open UnivalenceLemmas public</a>
<a id="41447" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="41450" class="Comment">-- open Univalence</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
